My mother, who is over 60, also got a few days of full rest after basically visiting Wuzhen a few days ago. It was enough to go out and stroll around for an hour every day during the few days of staying in Di Shang, so it can be said that every performance, activity, store, and every path were visited, and Di Shang Hotel was also visited.
Facilities: Comfortable standard room/king room. When checking in during the off-season, the weekend price is not low. The front desk arranged to upgrade the superior suite. Although the room price was several hundred cheaper on the day of the extension, the superior suite was still arranged to stay in the original room. The space is large, so everything is available. It just lacks windows. Except for the bathroom exhaust fan, there is no other ventilation method. For a new house that has been decorated for less than a year, the decoration smell is still difficult to dissipate. The mattress intelligent adjus**ent system of the king-size bed room can meet the different requirements of the mattress hardness for two people. The swimming pool is 1.2 meters, which is too shallow for adults. L'Occitane + Dyson Hotel exclusive custom-made model, perfect.
Hygiene: Very good, different cleaning staff, completely depends on the sense of responsibility.
Environment: Excellent. It is quiet at night, and there is no natural feeling of being awakened by the sound of birds at four or five o'clock when staying in Tong'an.
Service: Thoughtful and meticulous, the suitcase guy helped to call a car before leaving, and also helped to carry the luggage to the car. The usual consumables are replenished enough. The breakfast is extremely rich. On the third day of staying, I found that the types began to repeat, so it is likely to be a two-day cycle. The boys and girls at the front desk of the recreation service are very proactive and enthusiastic. There are people staying at any time to point out the direction for registration.
Double Xizha Scenic Area Tickets (You can enter and exit the Xizha Scenic Area multiple times during the stay until 12:00 on the day of departure): Self-funded plus extension, not used.
Welcome fruit: Three nights, there are slight differences. I love prunes the most.
First round of mini bar in the guest room: I have never had a concept of the term "first round". Staying in the same room for three consecutive days, should it be counted as three times according to the three single-day check-in orders, or only the first day of check-in is counted as one time. 4: As a newly opened hotel with a price of 2,000+, it is very cheap not to have an electric toilet.
5: The so-called luxurious view is the back of the scenic area, the Beijing-Hangzhou Grand Canal + a bunch of iron sheet factories and wasteland farmland, which completely overturned my original intention and impression of Wuzhen, and suddenly made me forget that I was in Wuzhen...
In summary, I was originally scheduled to stay for two nights, and I decisively returned to Yida Silk Industry on the second day.

msg:The hotel is located at the innermost of Wuzhen Scenic Area, with super five-star facilities and services. When entering the scenic area, you can check in, check in your luggage, and apply for facial recognition to enter the scenic area unlimited times at the special service desk in the visitor center. Turn right after entering the scenic area and there is a 24-hour free tour bus, which drives directly to the hotel. There is a doorman in the hotel lobby who takes the luggage, handles the room card, and introduces the hotel facilities along the way, and delivers it to the room, providing butler service throughout the whole process. The room is large and fully equipped, and the smart bed is specially introduced, so you can explore and experience it yourself. The breakfast in the morning is also very good, with many varieties. The whole accommodation experience is quite satisfactory. There is a tour bus at the lobby entrance where you want to go out of the hotel. If there is no car, tell the staff, they can call a car 24 hours a day. In the scenic area, you can see the nearest tourist station by looking at the Wuzhen Scenic Area Service Mini Program, and you can get on and off. The hotel also has a gym, an indoor swimming pool, and an infinity outdoor swimming pool. Compared with other hotels in the scenic area, I will stay here next time to experience top service and top facilities.

1. The hotel is modern, neat and clean, without the hassle of staying in an old building.

If you walk far, you can take the shuttle bus directly to the hotel door; or let the shuttle bus take you to the floating market first, and then go there again. Go shopping and come back; or you can take a shuttle bus to where you want to go, then walk to the pier and take the ferry back to the hotel. There are many ways to walk + transport, which is more convenient than living in the ancient town and only walking.
3. Breakfast is of high quality

shortcoming:
There is a gap in hotel pricing and service. I have stayed in many resort hotels. After experiencing the superior room plus scenic spot tickets this time, I compared it horizontally and found that the appropriate price range is 1,000-1,200. reason:
1. The facilities are average. It is obviously a new hotel, and there are almost no smart facilities. There are no smart toilets, smart speakers, or smart curtains (the curtains are considered semi-smart. They need to be pulled by hand first. One of the tacks fell off. Pulling the curtains directly scratched my hands. ), the TV is a Hisense and cannot project the screen and the sound effect is poor. There is a problem with the light control design. If you turn off the main control, you have to go to the door to turn on the toilet light. The only smart bed is the one that doesn't need to be smart at all. It will suddenly vibrate and then make a sound asking you to scan a QR code. It's very scary (but you can ask the waiter to turn it off).
2. The service is okay but not enthusiastic. At the beginning, there was no introduction to the hotel's activities, how to sign up, the facilities in the room, and whether the mini is free (if it had been introduced, I wouldn't have been shocked by the bed). I really had to do my homework on my own. , even if there is direct drinking water in the room, I only found out when I asked for bottled water. Waiters usually don't say hello when they walk by. Not to mention the services provided by the scenic area coordinator.
3. There are many breakfast categories but not many types. For example, cheese, yogurt, and salad can give you many choices, but they are all in one big category. Generally speaking, there are more cold food and less hot food, especially the freshly prepared hot food is not as good as many hotels of the same type.
